/*
Created07/07/2005
Modified07/07/2005
ProjectEMS National Dataset (NEMSIS)
AuthorWes Bowden
DatabaseMS SQL 2000 

---------------------------------------------------------------------
Updated 12/13/2007
Jorge Rojas
Changes:
Some NEMSIS elements were missing some of the NEMSIS Common NULL Values. These were add in.
Also the column DataElementVariableCode was changed from data type smallint to float because there are some codes that have a decimal
---------------------------------------------------------------------


Description:

This script will generate a table, create a view, and populate
the lookup values necessary to cross reference the data element
values with their descriptions.

!!! WARNING !!! This script will drop the objects if they are
already created. Please be sure you are applying
it to the correct database!
*/

-- Create TABLE: Element_to_Variable
PRINT 'Checking for Table: [Element_to_Variable]'
if exists (select * from dbo.sysobjects where id = object_id(N'[dbo].[Element_to_Variables]') and OBJECTPROPERTY(id, N'IsUserTable') = 1)
drop table [dbo].[Element_to_Variables]
GO
PRINT 'Done'
PRINT ''

PRINT 'Creating Table: [Element_to_Variable]'
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Element_to_Variables] (
[DataElementID] [int] IDENTITY (1, 1) NOT NULL ,
[DataElementNumber] [varchar] (10) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NOT NULL ,
[DataElementName] [varchar] (255) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL ,
[DataElementVariableCode] float NULL ,
[DataElementVariableName] [varchar] (255) COLLATE SQL_Latin1_General_CP1_CI_AS NULL 
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
PRINT 'Done'
PRINT ''

PRINT 'Creating Constraints for Table: [Element_to_Variable]'
ALTER TABLE [dbo].[Element_to_Variables] WITH NOCHECK ADD 
CONSTRAINT [PK_Element_to_Variables] PRIMARY KEY  CLUSTERED 
(
[DataElementID]
)  ON [PRIMARY] 
GO
PRINT 'Done'
PRINT ''

-- Create LookupValues View
PRINT 'Checking for View: [LookupValues]'
if exists (select * from dbo.sysobjects where id = object_id(N'[dbo].[LookupValues]') and OBJECTPROPERTY(id, N'IsView') = 1)
drop view [dbo].[LookupValues]
GO
PRINT 'Done'
PRINT ''

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON 
GO
SET ANSI_NULLS ON 
GO

PRINT 'Creating View: [LookupValues]'
GO
CREATE VIEW dbo.LookupValues
AS
SELECT DISTINCT DataElementVariableCode, DataElementVariableName
FROM         dbo.Element_to_Variables
WHERE     (NOT (DataElementVariableCode IS NULL))

GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER OFF 
GO
SET ANSI_NULLS ON 
GO
PRINT 'Done'
PRINT ''

-- Populate Values into Element_to_Variables Table 
SET NOCOUNT ON

 
PRINT 'Inserting 2576 records into Table: [Element_to_Variables]'
